Personally identifiable information may include, but is not limited to:&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Email Address&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">First and address), browser type, browser version, the pages of our Service that You visit, the time and date of Your visit, the time spent on those pages, unique device identifiers and other diagnostic data.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">When You access the Service by or through a mobile device, We may collect certain information automatically, including, but not limited to, the and other diagnostic data.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp;<br>We may also collect information that Your browser sends whenever You visit our Service or when You access the Service by or through a mobile device.&nbsp;</p><h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">Use of Your Personal Data</h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The Company may use Personal class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">To provide You with news, special offers and general information about other goods, services and events which we offer that are similar to those that you have necessary for the purposes set out in this Privacy Policy. We will retain and use Your Personal Data to the extent necessary to comply with our legal obligations (for example, if we are required to retain your data to comply with applicable laws), resolve disputes, and enforce our legal agreements and policies.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The Company will also retain Usage Data for internal analysis purposes. It means that this information may be transferred to — and maintained on — computers located outside of Your state, province, country or other governmental jurisdiction where the data protection laws may differ than those from Your jurisdiction.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Your consent to this Privacy Policy followed by Your submission of such information represents Your agreement to that transfer.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The Company will take all steps reasonably necessary to ensure that Your data is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy and no transfer of Your Personal Data will take place to an organization or a country unless there are adequate controls in place including the security of Your data and other personal information.&nbsp;</p><h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to erasure</h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">You have the right to request that we erase your personal data.
